# Text Elements
failure of one transaction causes
 several other dependent transactions
 to rollback or abort, ^JHZIFoL4

If in a schedule, ^ZYVNGwEo

Then such a schedule is called as
 a Cascading Schedule or 
Cascading Rollback or
 Cascading Abort. ^DgiVb8fh

The failure of transaction T 1 causes 
the transaction T 2 to rollback. ^U1qwBucY

The rollback of transaction T 2 causes
 the transaction T 3 to rollback. ^oio51zot

The rollback of transaction T 3 causes
 the transaction T 4 to rollback. ^SvskgJVs

A transaction is not allowed
 to read a data item until the
 last transaction 
that has written it 
is committed or aborted, ^hCQI2u6M

then such a schedule is 
called as a Cascadeless Schedule. ^hZmqVAUW

If in a schedule, ^mE7kmEA5

it allows uncommitted
write operations. ^qCFmHQCk

If in a schedule, ^4ZIFtEw7

A transaction is neither allowed to 
read nor write a data item 
until the last transaction that has written 
it is committed or aborted, ^nJMy0AvK

Then such a schedule 
is called as a Strict Schedule. ^CYo51sdh
